        <div class="title-quiz-choice my-3">
            <div class="font-weight-600">[Mai Hien key 6.0] - Reading part 4 - CULTURAL EXCHANGE</div>
            <div><h2 data-end="324" data-start="302"><span style="font-size:16px;">Read the passage quickly. Choose a heading for each numbered paragraph (1–7). There is one more heading than you need.</span></h2>

<h2 data-end="324" data-start="302"><span style="font-size:16px;">CULTURAL EXCHANGE</span></h2>

<p data-end="1363" data-start="326"><strong data-end="332" data-start="326">1.</strong><br data-end="335" data-start="332">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][0]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Redefining global cultural understanding ]</label><br data-end="657" data-start="654">
In today's interconnected world, global cultural understanding goes beyond simply learning about traditions and customs. It requires developing cultural intelligence—the ability to interpret behaviors, values, and communication styles in diverse contexts. While stereotypes once shaped international perceptions, cross-border collaborations now demand a more nuanced and adaptive mindset. Individuals must recognize that culture is dynamic rather than fixed, influenced by globalization, migration, and technological change. Redefining cultural understanding means moving away from superficial knowledge and adopting a deeper appreciation of shared human experiences while respecting distinct identities.</p>

<p data-end="2435" data-start="1365"><strong data-end="1371" data-start="1365">2.</strong><br data-end="1374" data-start="1371">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][1]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Encouraging cross-cultural festivals ]</label><br data-end="1696" data-start="1693">
Cross-cultural festivals play a pivotal role in fostering inclusivity and unity among diverse populations. These events provide a platform where communities can showcase their art, music, cuisine, and heritage, encouraging meaningful dialogue and mutual appreciation. More importantly, they create opportunities for participants to interact directly, dismantling prejudices and stereotypes through firsthand experiences. Governments and cultural organizations increasingly recognize the educational and economic value of such festivals, supporting them to enhance social cohesion. When managed effectively, cross-cultural festivals not only celebrate diversity but also build stronger, more resilient communities in a globalized society.</p>

<p data-end="3478" data-start="2437"><strong data-end="2443" data-start="2437">3.</strong><br data-end="2446" data-start="2443">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Promoting language exchange programs ]</label><br data-end="2768" data-start="2765">
Language exchange programs are one of the most effective tools for promoting intercultural communication and understanding. By enabling learners to practice directly with native speakers, these initiatives help participants grasp cultural nuances, including humor, idioms, and nonverbal cues that textbooks often overlook. Moreover, such programs cultivate empathy by allowing individuals to experience another culture's perspective on identity, history, and values. With the rise of virtual platforms, international exchanges are becoming more accessible and affordable, empowering students and professionals alike to develop cross-cultural competence—a critical skill in education, business, and diplomacy.</p>

<p data-end="4580" data-start="3480"><strong data-end="3486" data-start="3480">4.</strong><br data-end="3489" data-start="3486">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][3]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Overemphasis on commercial tourism ]</label><br data-end="3811" data-start="3808">
While tourism promotes economic growth, its over-commercialization often undermines authentic cultural exchange. Popular destinations risk being transformed into commodified attractions, where traditions are staged to meet tourists' expectations rather than reflecting genuine practices. This phenomenon can lead to the erosion of local identity and the homogenization of cultural experiences. Travelers seeking authenticity may instead encounter curated performances and mass-produced souvenirs. To counter this, policymakers and tourism boards must balance economic benefits with cultural integrity, prioritizing sustainable tourism models that respect local communities, preserve heritage, and encourage more meaningful interactions between visitors and residents.</p>

<p data-end="5660" data-start="4582"><strong data-end="4588" data-start="4582">5.</strong><br data-end="4591" data-start="4588">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Concerns about cultural preservation ]</label><br data-end="4913" data-start="4910">
Globalization and rapid urbanization have intensified concerns about the loss of intangible cultural heritage. Languages, rituals, folk traditions, and crafts are disappearing at alarming rates as younger generations adopt global trends. While modernization brings convenience and economic opportunities, it also risks creating cultural homogenization. Governments, educators, and community leaders must collaborate on initiatives that document, protect, and revitalize endangered traditions. Technology can play a vital role, from digitizing ancient manuscripts to creating virtual museums. Preserving culture is not about resisting change but maintaining diversity, ensuring that global progress does not come at the cost of cultural richness.</p>

<p data-end="6697" data-start="5662"><strong data-end="5668" data-start="5662">6.</strong><br data-end="5671" data-start="5668">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][5]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Building mutual respect among communities ]</label><br data-end="5993" data-start="5990">
True cultural exchange thrives only when grounded in mutual respect and empathy. Communities must move beyond tolerance and strive for genuine understanding of each other's values, beliefs, and histories. Prejudices often stem from ignorance, and open dialogue can dismantle misconceptions while fostering collaboration. Educational institutions, media, and public policies have the power to promote inclusive narratives that highlight common humanity rather than differences. By recognizing that cultural diversity strengthens societies, individuals and communities can build trust-based relationships that lead to cooperation in addressing global challenges, from climate change to social inequality.</p>

<p data-end="7758" data-start="6699"><strong data-end="6705" data-start="6699">7.</strong><br data-end="6708" data-start="6705">
<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0ff7be275cbfaad8b4574][answer][6]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building mutual respect among communities">Building mutual respect among communities</option><option value="Concerns about cultural preservation">Concerns about cultural preservation</option><option value="Encouraging cross-cultural festivals">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</option><option value="Focusing on authentic cultural experiences">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</option><option value="Overemphasis on commercial tourism">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</option><option value="Promoting language exchange programs">Promoting language exchange programs</option><option value="Promoting personal travel blogs">Promoting personal travel blogs</option><option value="Redefining global cultural understanding">Redefining global cultural understanding</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Focusing on authentic cultural experiences ]</label><br data-end="7030" data-start="7027">
As globalization reshapes travel and lifestyle choices, there is a growing demand for authentic cultural experiences. Travelers increasingly seek opportunities to engage with local communities, learn traditional crafts, and participate in everyday cultural practices rather than consuming staged performances. Authenticity, however, requires sensitivity and humility: visitors must approach new cultures as learners, not consumers. Meanwhile, communities hosting tourists should feel empowered to share their heritage on their own terms. Prioritizing authenticity transforms cultural exchange from a passive observation into an immersive, transformative experience that fosters deeper understanding and meaningful connections.</p></div>
        </div>

<h2 data-end="349" data-start="318"><em>Giải thích cụ thể</em></h2>

<h2 data-end="349" data-start="318">CULTURAL EXCHANGE (Giao lưu văn hóa)</h2>

<h3 data-end="404" data-start="351">1. <strong data-end="402" data-start="358">Redefining global cultural understanding</strong></h3>

<p data-end="455" data-start="405">(<em data-end="452" data-start="406">Định nghĩa lại sự thấu hiểu văn hóa toàn cầu</em>)</p>

<p data-end="813" data-start="457">In today's interconnected world, <strong data-end="523" data-start="490">global cultural understanding</strong> goes beyond simply learning about traditions and customs. It requires developing <strong data-end="630" data-start="605">cultural intelligence</strong>… Redefining cultural understanding means moving away from superficial knowledge and adopting a deeper appreciation of shared human experiences while respecting distinct identities.</p>

<p data-end="1188" data-start="815"><em data-end="1186" data-start="815">Trong thế giới ngày nay, <strong data-end="874" data-start="841">sự thấu hiểu văn hóa toàn cầu</strong> không chỉ dừng lại ở việc tìm hiểu phong tục và truyền thống. Nó đòi hỏi phải phát triển <strong data-end="983" data-start="964">trí tuệ văn hóa</strong>... <strong data-end="1026" data-start="987">Định nghĩa lại sự thấu hiểu văn hóa</strong> có nghĩa là từ bỏ sự hiểu biết hời hợt và thay vào đó là trân trọng sâu sắc hơn những trải nghiệm chung của con người, đồng thời tôn trọng bản sắc riêng biệt.</em></p>

<p data-end="1329" data-start="1190"><strong data-end="1205" data-start="1190">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn nói rõ đến việc <strong data-end="1267" data-start="1231">định nghĩa lại cách hiểu văn hóa</strong> trong thời đại toàn cầu hóa, nên tiêu đề hoàn toàn phù hợp.</p>

<h3 data-end="1385" data-start="1336">2. <strong data-end="1383" data-start="1343">Encouraging cross-cultural festivals</strong></h3>

<p data-end="1426" data-start="1386">(<em data-end="1423" data-start="1387">Khuyến khích các lễ hội đa văn hóa</em>)</p>

<p data-end="1644" data-start="1428"><strong data-end="1456" data-start="1428">Cross-cultural festivals</strong> play a pivotal role in fostering inclusivity and unity among diverse populations. These events provide a platform where communities can showcase their art, music, cuisine, and heritage…</p>

<p data-end="1873" data-start="1646"><em data-end="1871" data-start="1646"><strong data-end="1672" data-start="1647">Các lễ hội đa văn hóa</strong> đóng vai trò quan trọng trong việc thúc đẩy sự hòa nhập và đoàn kết giữa nhiều cộng đồng khác nhau. Những sự kiện này là nơi để cộng đồng giới thiệu nghệ thuật, âm nhạc, ẩm thực và di sản của mình…</em></p>

<p data-end="1985" data-start="1875"><strong data-end="1890" data-start="1875">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề khớp vì toàn đoạn tập trung nói về vai trò và lợi ích của <strong data-end="1982" data-start="1957">các lễ hội đa văn hóa</strong>.</p>

<h3 data-end="2041" data-start="1992">3. <strong data-end="2039" data-start="1999">Promoting language exchange programs</strong></h3>

<p data-end="2091" data-start="2042">(<em data-end="2088" data-start="2043">Thúc đẩy các chương trình trao đổi ngôn ngữ</em>)</p>

<p data-end="2296" data-start="2093"><strong data-end="2123" data-start="2093">Language exchange programs</strong> are one of the most effective tools for promoting intercultural communication… They help participants grasp cultural nuances, including humor, idioms, and nonverbal cues…</p>

<p data-end="2538" data-start="2298"><em data-end="2536" data-start="2298"><strong data-end="2337" data-start="2299">Các chương trình trao đổi ngôn ngữ</strong> là một trong những công cụ hiệu quả nhất để thúc đẩy giao tiếp liên văn hóa… Chúng giúp người học nắm bắt được sự tinh tế trong văn hóa, bao gồm sự hài hước, thành ngữ và các tín hiệu phi ngôn ngữ…</em></p>

<p data-end="2662" data-start="2540"><strong data-end="2555" data-start="2540">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn tập trung nói đến lợi ích của <strong data-end="2633" data-start="2595">các chương trình trao đổi ngôn ngữ</strong>, nên tiêu đề là chính xác.</p>

<h3 data-end="2716" data-start="2669">4. <strong data-end="2714" data-start="2676">Overemphasis on commercial tourism</strong></h3>

<p data-end="2766" data-start="2717">(<em data-end="2763" data-start="2718">Sự nhấn mạnh quá mức vào du lịch thương mại</em>)</p>

<p data-end="2960" data-start="2768">While tourism promotes economic growth, its <strong data-end="2838" data-start="2812">over-commercialization</strong> often undermines authentic cultural exchange. Popular destinations risk being transformed into commodified attractions…</p>

<p data-end="3175" data-start="2962"><em data-end="3173" data-start="2962">Mặc dù du lịch thúc đẩy tăng trưởng kinh tế, nhưng <strong data-end="3043" data-start="3014">sự thương mại hóa quá mức</strong> thường làm suy yếu sự trao đổi văn hóa chân thực. Các điểm đến nổi tiếng có nguy cơ bị biến thành những sản phẩm thương mại hóa…</em></p>

<p data-end="3317" data-start="3177"><strong data-end="3192" data-start="3177">Giải thích:</strong> Nội dung cảnh báo về việc <strong data-end="3253" data-start="3219">du lịch thương mại hóa quá mức</strong>, khiến trải nghiệm văn hóa mất tính chân thực → khớp tiêu đề.</p>

<h3 data-end="3373" data-start="3324">5. <strong data-end="3371" data-start="3331">Concerns about cultural preservation</strong></h3>

<p data-end="3417" data-start="3374">(<em data-end="3414" data-start="3375">Những lo ngại về việc bảo tồn văn hóa</em>)</p>

<p data-end="3601" data-start="3419">Globalization and rapid urbanization have intensified <strong data-end="3532" data-start="3473">concerns about the loss of intangible cultural heritage</strong>. Languages, rituals, folk traditions, and crafts are disappearing…</p>

<p data-end="3798" data-start="3603"><em data-end="3796" data-start="3603">Toàn cầu hóa và đô thị hóa nhanh chóng đã làm gia tăng <strong data-end="3721" data-start="3659">những lo ngại về sự mất mát của di sản văn hóa phi vật thể</strong>. Ngôn ngữ, nghi lễ, truyền thống dân gian và nghề thủ công đang biến mất…</em></p>

<p data-end="3905" data-start="3800"><strong data-end="3815" data-start="3800">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn này nói rõ ràng đến <strong data-end="3879" data-start="3841">sự lo ngại về việc bảo tồn văn hóa</strong>, nên tiêu đề khớp nhất.</p>

<h3 data-end="3966" data-start="3912">6. <strong data-end="3964" data-start="3919">Building mutual respect among communities</strong></h3>

<p data-end="4022" data-start="3967">(<em data-end="4019" data-start="3968">Xây dựng sự tôn trọng lẫn nhau giữa các cộng đồng</em>)</p>

<p data-end="4187" data-start="4024">True cultural exchange thrives only when grounded in <strong data-end="4095" data-start="4077">mutual respect</strong> and empathy. Communities must move beyond tolerance and strive for genuine understanding…</p>

<p data-end="4375" data-start="4189"><em data-end="4373" data-start="4189">Sự trao đổi văn hóa thực sự chỉ phát triển khi dựa trên <strong data-end="4271" data-start="4246">sự tôn trọng lẫn nhau</strong> và sự thấu cảm. Các cộng đồng phải vượt ra khỏi mức độ khoan dung và hướng tới sự thấu hiểu thực sự…</em></p>

<p data-end="4505" data-start="4377"><strong data-end="4392" data-start="4377">Giải thích:</strong> Toàn đoạn nhấn mạnh rằng trao đổi văn hóa phải dựa trên <strong data-end="4474" data-start="4449">sự tôn trọng lẫn nhau</strong>, rất trùng khớp với tiêu đề.</p>

<h3 data-end="4567" data-start="4512">7. <strong data-end="4565" data-start="4519">Focusing on authentic cultural experiences</strong></h3>

<p data-end="4623" data-start="4568">(<em data-end="4620" data-start="4569">Tập trung vào những trải nghiệm văn hóa chân thực</em>)</p>

<p data-end="4833" data-start="4625">There is a growing demand for <strong data-end="4689" data-start="4655">authentic cultural experiences</strong>. Travelers increasingly seek opportunities to engage with local communities, learn traditional crafts, and participate in everyday practices…</p>

<p data-end="5043" data-start="4835"><em data-end="5041" data-start="4835">Ngày càng có nhiều nhu cầu về <strong data-end="4905" data-start="4866">những trải nghiệm văn hóa chân thực</strong>. Du khách muốn được tham gia trực tiếp với cộng đồng địa phương, học nghề thủ công truyền thống, và hòa mình vào đời sống thường nhật…</em></p>

<p data-end="5171" data-start="5045"><strong data-end="5060" data-start="5045">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn nói rõ ràng đến xu hướng tập trung vào <strong data-end="5138" data-start="5105">trải nghiệm văn hóa chân thực</strong>, nên tiêu đề này phù hợp nhất.</p>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

<p data-end="1222" data-start="460"><strong data-end="780" data-start="460">1. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][0]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Redefining holistic health approaches ]</label></strong><br data-end="783" data-start="780">

Holistic views highlight the <strong data-end="920" data-start="906">connection</strong> between the <strong data-end="964" data-start="933">body, mind, and environment</strong>, urging people to also consider <strong data-end="1061" data-start="997">emotional balance, mental focus, nutrition, and daily habits</strong>. <p data-end="2014" data-start="1229"><strong data-end="1549" data-start="1229">2. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][1]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Promoting mental health awareness ]</label></strong><br data-end="1552" data-start="1549">
<strong data-end="1569" data-start="1552">Mental health</strong> is becoming a central topic in <strong data-end="1618" data-start="1601">public health</strong> discussions. Awareness efforts work to <strong data-end="1675" data-start="1658">reduce stigma</strong> linked to <strong data-end="1704" data-start="1686">mental illness</strong> and motivate people to speak more <strong data-end="1749" data-start="1739">openly</strong> about their difficulties. By teaching communities to recognize <strong data-end="1862" data-start="1813">early signs of anxiety, depression, or stress</strong>, individuals are encouraged to seek help faster. Many organizations now provide <strong data-end="1962" data-start="1943">support systems</strong> and <strong data-end="1980" data-start="1967">resources</strong> to build a more caring society.</p>

<p data-end="2785" data-start="2021"><strong data-end="2341" data-start="2021">3. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Encouraging community fitness programs ]</label></strong><br data-end="2344" data-start="2341">
<strong data-end="2376" data-start="2344">Community fitness activities</strong> are increasingly popular as a way to make <strong data-end="2431" data-start="2419">exercise</strong> more enjoyable and accessible. Joining <strong data-end="2487" data-start="2471">group events</strong> like <strong data-end="2543" data-start="2493">yoga sessions, walking groups, or sports teams</strong> not only improves <strong data-end="2583" data-start="2562">physical strength</strong> but also builds <strong data-end="2622" data-start="2600">social connections</strong>. <p data-end="3608" data-start="2792"><strong data-end="3112" data-start="2792">4. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][3]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Overemphasis on trendy diets ]</label></strong><br data-end="3115" data-start="3112">

Building a healthy <strong data-end="3540" data-start="3519">food relationship</strong> is ultimately more valuable than following the newest diet trend.</p>

<p data-end="4308" data-start="3615"><strong data-end="3935" data-start="3615">5. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Concerns about wellness misinformation ]</label></strong><br data-end="3938" data-start="3935">
The growth of <strong data-end="3968" data-start="3952">social media</strong> has spread a lot of <strong data-end="4011" data-start="3989">health information</strong>, but not all of it is <strong data-end="4046" data-start="4034">accurate</strong>. False claims about <strong data-end="4109" data-start="4067">supplements, treatments, and practices</strong> can cause <strong data-end="4133" data-start="4120">confusion</strong> or even <strong data-end="4150" data-start="4142">harm</strong>. Individuals need to <strong data-end="4202" data-start="4172">evaluate sources carefully</strong>, consult <strong data-end="4230" data-start="4212">health experts</strong>, and follow <strong data-end="4268" data-start="4243">evidence-based advice</strong> when shaping their wellness routines.</p>

<p data-end="5024" data-start="4315"><strong data-end="4635" data-start="4315">6. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][5]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Building supportive health communities ]</label></strong><br data-end="4638" data-start="4635">
Supportive <strong data-end="4668" data-start="4649">wellness groups</strong> have a big role in maintaining <strong data-end="4722" data-start="4700">healthy lifestyles</strong>. Whether online forums or local <strong data-end="4766" data-start="4755">meetups</strong>, these communities offer <strong data-end="4841" data-start="4792">encouragement, accountability, and motivation</strong>. <p data-end="5716" data-start="5031"><strong data-end="5351" data-start="5031">7. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c10450e275cb755d8b4588][answer][6]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Building supportive health communities">Building supportive health communities</option><option value="Concerns about wellness misinformation">Concerns about wellness misinformation</option><option value="Encouraging community fitness programs">Encouraging community fitness programs</option><option value="Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes">Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes</option><option value="Overemphasis on trendy diets">Overemphasis on trendy diets</option><option value="Promoting mental health awareness">Promoting mental health awareness</option><option value="Redefining holistic health approaches">Redefining holistic health approaches</option><option value="Rising demand for digital wellness tools">Rising demand for digital wellness tools</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes ]</label></strong><br data-end="5354" data-start="5351">
Long-term <strong data-end="5376" data-start="5364">wellness</strong> requires more than just <strong data-end="5420" data-start="5401">temporary diets</strong> or short bursts of <strong data-end="5452" data-start="5440">exercise</strong>. It depends on <strong data-end="5490" data-start="5468">sustainable habits</strong> like better <strong data-end="5512" data-start="5503">sleep</strong>, stress management, and regular physical activity. By setting <strong data-end="5594" data-start="5575">realistic goals</strong> and making gradual adjustments, individuals are more likely to enjoy lasting benefits and a higher <strong data-end="5713" data-start="5694">quality of life</strong>.</p></div>

<hr data-end="86" data-start="83">
<h3 data-end="190" data-start="88">1. Redefining holistic health approaches (<em data-end="187" data-start="134">Định nghĩa lại các cách tiếp cận sức khỏe toàn diện</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="650" data-start="191">In recent years, the meaning of <strong data-end="233" data-start="223">health</strong> has broadened beyond only <strong data-end="283" data-start="260">physical well-being</strong>. <strong data-end="303" data-start="285">Holistic views</strong> highlight the connection between the <strong data-end="349" data-start="341">body</strong>, <strong data-end="359" data-start="351">mind</strong>, and <strong data-end="380" data-start="365">environment</strong>, urging people to also consider <strong data-end="434" data-start="413">emotional balance</strong>, <strong data-end="452" data-start="436">mental focus</strong>, <strong data-end="467" data-start="454">nutrition</strong>, and <strong data-end="489" data-start="473">daily habits</strong>. This wider outlook allows individuals to gain <strong data-end="562" data-start="537">long-lasting wellness</strong> by addressing multiple <strong data-end="605" data-start="586">aspects of life</strong> instead of treating separate <strong data-end="647" data-start="635">symptoms</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="1141" data-start="652"><em data-end="1139" data-start="652">(Trong những năm gần đây, ý nghĩa của <strong data-end="703" data-start="691">sức khỏe</strong> đã mở rộng vượt xa chỉ là <strong data-end="751" data-start="730">sức khỏe thể chất</strong>. Quan điểm <strong data-end="776" data-start="763">toàn diện</strong> nhấn mạnh sự kết nối giữa <strong data-end="813" data-start="803">cơ thể</strong>, <strong data-end="826" data-start="815">tâm trí</strong> và <strong data-end="844" data-start="830">môi trường</strong>, kêu gọi mọi người chú ý đến <strong data-end="894" data-start="874">cân bằng cảm xúc</strong>, <strong data-end="919" data-start="896">tập trung tinh thần</strong>, <strong data-end="935" data-start="921">dinh dưỡng</strong> và <strong data-end="962" data-start="939">thói quen hàng ngày</strong>. Cách nhìn rộng hơn này giúp mỗi cá nhân đạt được <strong data-end="1034" data-start="1013">sức khỏe bền vững</strong> bằng cách giải quyết nhiều <strong data-end="1089" data-start="1062">khía cạnh của cuộc sống</strong> thay vì chỉ xử lý các <strong data-end="1127" data-start="1112">triệu chứng</strong> riêng lẻ.)</em></p>

<p data-end="1266" data-start="1143"><strong data-end="1158" data-start="1143">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn nói về việc sức khỏe được hiểu rộng hơn, nhấn mạnh cách tiếp cận toàn diện, nên tiêu đề phù hợp.</p>

<hr data-end="1271" data-start="1268">
<h3 data-end="1360" data-start="1273">2. Promoting mental health awareness (<em data-end="1357" data-start="1315">Thúc đẩy nhận thức về sức khỏe tinh thần</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="1855" data-start="1361"><strong data-end="1378" data-start="1361">Mental health</strong> is becoming a central <strong data-end="1410" data-start="1401">topic</strong> in public health discussions. <strong data-end="1462" data-start="1441">Awareness efforts</strong> work to reduce <strong data-end="1488" data-start="1478">stigma</strong> linked to <strong data-end="1517" data-start="1499">mental illness</strong> and motivate people to speak more openly about their <strong data-end="1587" data-start="1571">difficulties</strong>. By teaching <strong data-end="1616" data-start="1601">communities</strong> to recognize early <strong data-end="1645" data-start="1636">signs</strong> of <strong data-end="1660" data-start="1649">anxiety</strong>, <strong data-end="1676" data-start="1662">depression</strong>, or <strong data-end="1691" data-start="1681">stress</strong>, individuals are encouraged to <strong data-end="1736" data-start="1723">seek help</strong> faster. Many <strong data-end="1767" data-start="1750">organizations</strong> now provide <strong data-end="1799" data-start="1780">support systems</strong> and <strong data-end="1817" data-start="1804">resources</strong> to build a more <strong data-end="1852" data-start="1834">caring society</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="2412" data-start="1857"><em data-end="2410" data-start="1857">(<strong data-end="1881" data-start="1859">Sức khỏe tinh thần</strong> đang trở thành một <strong data-end="1911" data-start="1901">chủ đề</strong> trung tâm trong các cuộc thảo luận về y tế cộng đồng. Các nỗ lực nâng cao <strong data-end="1999" data-start="1986">nhận thức</strong> giúp giảm <strong data-end="2020" data-start="2010">kỳ thị</strong> liên quan đến <strong data-end="2050" data-start="2035">bệnh tâm lý</strong> và khuyến khích mọi người cởi mở hơn về <strong data-end="2103" data-start="2091">khó khăn</strong> của mình. Bằng cách dạy cho <strong data-end="2145" data-start="2132">cộng đồng</strong> nhận biết các <strong data-end="2172" data-start="2160">dấu hiệu</strong> sớm của <strong data-end="2190" data-start="2181">lo âu</strong>, <strong data-end="2204" data-start="2192">trầm cảm</strong> hay <strong data-end="2223" data-start="2209">căng thẳng</strong>, mỗi cá nhân được khuyến khích <strong data-end="2278" data-start="2255">tìm kiếm sự giúp đỡ</strong> nhanh hơn. Nhiều <strong data-end="2307" data-start="2296">tổ chức</strong> hiện nay cũng cung cấp <strong data-end="2350" data-start="2331">hệ thống hỗ trợ</strong> và <strong data-end="2367" data-start="2354">nguồn lực</strong> để xây dựng một xã hội <strong data-end="2403" data-start="2391">quan tâm</strong> hơn.)</em></p>

<p data-end="2533" data-start="2414"><strong data-end="2429" data-start="2414">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn tập trung vào nâng cao ý thức cộng đồng về sức khỏe tinh thần, nên tiêu đề này phù hợp nhất.</p>

<hr data-end="2538" data-start="2535">
<h3 data-end="2639" data-start="2540">3. Encouraging community fitness programs (<em data-end="2636" data-start="2587">Khuyến khích các chương trình thể dục cộng đồng</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="3117" data-start="2640"><strong data-end="2672" data-start="2640">Community fitness activities</strong> are increasingly <strong data-end="2701" data-start="2690">popular</strong> as a way to make <strong data-end="2731" data-start="2719">exercise</strong> more <strong data-end="2750" data-start="2737">enjoyable</strong> and <strong data-end="2769" data-start="2755">accessible</strong>. Joining <strong data-end="2795" data-start="2779">group events</strong> like <strong data-end="2818" data-start="2801">yoga sessions</strong>, <strong data-end="2838" data-start="2820">walking groups</strong>, or <strong data-end="2859" data-start="2843">sports teams</strong> not only improves <strong data-end="2899" data-start="2878">physical strength</strong> but also builds <strong data-end="2938" data-start="2916">social connections</strong>. Such programs create a sense of <strong data-end="2985" data-start="2972">belonging</strong> and help people remain <strong data-end="3023" data-start="3009">consistent</strong> with their <strong data-end="3054" data-start="3035">fitness journey</strong>, leading to <strong data-end="3080" data-start="3067">healthier</strong> and more <strong data-end="3114" data-start="3090">positive communities</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="3628" data-start="3119"><em data-end="3626" data-start="3119">(Các <strong data-end="3156" data-start="3125">hoạt động thể dục cộng đồng</strong> ngày càng trở nên <strong data-end="3187" data-start="3175">phổ biến</strong> như một cách để khiến việc <strong data-end="3228" data-start="3215">tập luyện</strong> trở nên <strong data-end="3247" data-start="3237">thú vị</strong> và <strong data-end="3266" data-start="3251">dễ tiếp cận</strong> hơn. Tham gia các <strong data-end="3301" data-start="3285">sự kiện nhóm</strong> như <strong data-end="3318" data-start="3306">lớp yoga</strong>, <strong data-end="3340" data-start="3320">câu lạc bộ đi bộ</strong>, hoặc <strong data-end="3363" data-start="3347">đội thể thao</strong> không chỉ cải thiện <strong data-end="3405" data-start="3384">sức khỏe thể chất</strong> mà còn xây dựng <strong data-end="3445" data-start="3422">mối liên kết xã hội</strong>. Những chương trình này tạo ra cảm giác <strong data-end="3497" data-start="3486">gắn kết</strong> và giúp mọi người duy trì sự <strong data-end="3540" data-start="3527">kiên định</strong> với <strong data-end="3569" data-start="3545">hành trình tập luyện</strong>, mang đến cộng đồng <strong data-end="3603" data-start="3590">khỏe mạnh</strong> và <strong data-end="3619" data-start="3607">tích cực</strong> hơn.)</em></p>

<p data-end="3736" data-start="3630"><strong data-end="3645" data-start="3630">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn mô tả lợi ích của các hoạt động thể chất tập thể, nên tiêu đề này là chính xác.</p>

<hr data-end="3741" data-start="3738">
<h3 data-end="3830" data-start="3743">4. Overemphasis on trendy diets (<em data-end="3827" data-start="3780">Quá chú trọng vào các chế độ ăn theo xu hướng</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="4360" data-start="3831">Although many <strong data-end="3858" data-start="3845">fad diets</strong> claim to bring quick <strong data-end="3895" data-start="3880">weight loss</strong> or better <strong data-end="3916" data-start="3906">health</strong>, depending too much on them can be <strong data-end="3961" data-start="3952">risky</strong>. Some famous <strong data-end="3984" data-start="3975">diets</strong> lack <strong data-end="4012" data-start="3990">scientific support</strong> and may cut out <strong data-end="4052" data-start="4029">essential nutrients</strong>, causing <strong data-end="4086" data-start="4062">imbalanced nutrition</strong>. <strong data-end="4099" data-start="4088">Experts</strong> highlight that sustainable <strong data-end="4137" data-start="4127">eating</strong> means focusing on <strong data-end="4174" data-start="4156">balanced meals</strong>, <strong data-end="4190" data-start="4176">moderation</strong>, and <strong data-end="4214" data-start="4196">personal needs</strong> instead of <strong data-end="4246" data-start="4226">short-term fixes</strong>. Building a <strong data-end="4288" data-start="4259">healthy food relationship</strong> is ultimately more valuable than following the newest <strong data-end="4357" data-start="4343">diet trend</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="4975" data-start="4362"><em data-end="4973" data-start="4362">(Mặc dù nhiều <strong data-end="4394" data-start="4377">chế độ ăn mốt</strong> tuyên bố giúp <strong data-end="4421" data-start="4409">giảm cân</strong> nhanh hoặc cải thiện <strong data-end="4455" data-start="4443">sức khỏe</strong>, nhưng dựa dẫm quá nhiều vào chúng có thể <strong data-end="4511" data-start="4498">nguy hiểm</strong>. Một số <strong data-end="4533" data-start="4520">chế độ ăn</strong> nổi tiếng thiếu <strong data-end="4568" data-start="4550">cơ sở khoa học</strong> và có thể loại bỏ các <strong data-end="4620" data-start="4591">chất dinh dưỡng thiết yếu</strong>, gây <strong data-end="4653" data-start="4626">mất cân bằng dinh dưỡng</strong>. Các <strong data-end="4673" data-start="4659">chuyên gia</strong> nhấn mạnh rằng việc <strong data-end="4705" data-start="4694">ăn uống</strong> bền vững có nghĩa là tập trung vào <strong data-end="4759" data-start="4741">bữa ăn cân đối</strong>, <strong data-end="4772" data-start="4761">điều độ</strong>, và phù hợp với <strong data-end="4808" data-start="4789">nhu cầu cá nhân</strong> thay vì các giải pháp <strong data-end="4843" data-start="4831">ngắn hạn</strong>. Xây dựng một <strong data-end="4897" data-start="4858">mối quan hệ lành mạnh với thực phẩm</strong> cuối cùng có giá trị hơn là chạy theo các <strong data-end="4961" data-start="4940">xu hướng ăn kiêng</strong> mới nhất.)</em></p>

<p data-end="5086" data-start="4977"><strong data-end="4992" data-start="4977">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn cảnh báo về sự lạm dụng chế độ ăn theo trào lưu, vì vậy tiêu đề này rất chính xác.</p>

<hr data-end="5091" data-start="5088">
<h3 data-end="5198" data-start="5093">5. Concerns about wellness misinformation (<em data-end="5195" data-start="5140">Lo ngại về thông tin sai lệch trong lĩnh vực sức khỏe</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="5589" data-start="5199">The growth of <strong data-end="5229" data-start="5213">social media</strong> has spread a lot of <strong data-end="5272" data-start="5250">health information</strong>, but not all of it is <strong data-end="5307" data-start="5295">accurate</strong>. <strong data-end="5325" data-start="5309">False claims</strong> about <strong data-end="5347" data-start="5332">supplements</strong>, <strong data-end="5363" data-start="5349">treatments</strong>, and <strong data-end="5382" data-start="5369">practices</strong> can cause <strong data-end="5406" data-start="5393">confusion</strong> or even <strong data-end="5423" data-start="5415">harm</strong>. <strong data-end="5440" data-start="5425">Individuals</strong> need to <strong data-end="5469" data-start="5449">evaluate sources</strong> carefully, <strong data-end="5507" data-start="5481">consult health experts</strong>, and follow <strong data-end="5545" data-start="5520">evidence-based advice</strong> when shaping their <strong data-end="5586" data-start="5565">wellness routines</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="6063" data-start="5591"><em data-end="6061" data-start="5591">(Sự phát triển của <strong data-end="5626" data-start="5611">mạng xã hội</strong> đã lan truyền rất nhiều <strong data-end="5673" data-start="5651">thông tin sức khỏe</strong>, nhưng không phải tất cả đều <strong data-end="5716" data-start="5703">chính xác</strong>. Những <strong data-end="5745" data-start="5724">tuyên bố sai lệch</strong> về <strong data-end="5770" data-start="5749">thực phẩm bổ sung</strong>, <strong data-end="5796" data-start="5772">phương pháp điều trị</strong> và <strong data-end="5813" data-start="5800">thực hành</strong> có thể gây <strong data-end="5837" data-start="5825">nhầm lẫn</strong> hoặc thậm chí <strong data-end="5863" data-start="5852">tổn hại</strong>. <strong data-end="5880" data-start="5865">Mỗi cá nhân</strong> cần <strong data-end="5913" data-start="5885">đánh giá nguồn thông tin</strong> cẩn thận, <strong data-end="5960" data-start="5924">tham khảo ý kiến chuyên gia y tế</strong>, và tuân theo các <strong data-end="6013" data-start="5979">lời khuyên dựa trên bằng chứng</strong> khi xây dựng <strong data-end="6058" data-start="6027">thói quen chăm sóc sức khỏe</strong>.)</em></p>

<p data-end="6181" data-start="6065"><strong data-end="6080" data-start="6065">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn nhấn mạnh sự nguy hiểm của thông tin sai lệch về sức khỏe, nên tiêu đề hoàn toàn phù hợp.</p>

<hr data-end="6186" data-start="6183">
<h3 data-end="6274" data-start="6188">6. Building supportive health communities (<em data-end="6271" data-start="6235">Xây dựng cộng đồng hỗ trợ sức khỏe</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="6701" data-start="6275"><strong data-end="6305" data-start="6275">Supportive wellness groups</strong> have a big role in maintaining <strong data-end="6359" data-start="6337">healthy lifestyles</strong>. Whether <strong data-end="6386" data-start="6369">online forums</strong> or <strong data-end="6407" data-start="6390">local meetups</strong>, these <strong data-end="6430" data-start="6415">communities</strong> offer <strong data-end="6454" data-start="6437">encouragement</strong>, <strong data-end="6474" data-start="6456">accountability</strong>, and <strong data-end="6494" data-start="6480">motivation</strong>. <strong data-end="6507" data-start="6496">Members</strong> can <strong data-end="6533" data-start="6512">share experiences</strong>, <strong data-end="6557" data-start="6535">celebrate progress</strong>, and find <strong data-end="6580" data-start="6568">strength</strong> during <strong data-end="6602" data-start="6588">challenges</strong>. Such an <strong data-end="6627" data-start="6612">environment</strong> empowers people to achieve their <strong data-end="6677" data-start="6661">health goals</strong> more <strong data-end="6698" data-start="6683">effectively</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="7172" data-start="6703"><em data-end="7170" data-start="6703">(Các <strong data-end="6733" data-start="6709">nhóm hỗ trợ sức khỏe</strong> đóng vai trò quan trọng trong việc duy trì <strong data-end="6799" data-start="6777">lối sống lành mạnh</strong>. Dù là <strong data-end="6830" data-start="6807">diễn đàn trực tuyến</strong> hay <strong data-end="6856" data-start="6835">gặp mặt trực tiếp</strong>, những <strong data-end="6877" data-start="6864">cộng đồng</strong> này mang lại sự <strong data-end="6906" data-start="6894">khích lệ</strong>, <strong data-end="6923" data-start="6908">trách nhiệm</strong> và <strong data-end="6939" data-start="6927">động lực</strong>. <strong data-end="6959" data-start="6941">Các thành viên</strong> có thể <strong data-end="6990" data-start="6967">chia sẻ trải nghiệm</strong>, <strong data-end="7011" data-start="6992">ăn mừng tiến bộ</strong>, và tìm thấy <strong data-end="7037" data-start="7025">sức mạnh</strong> khi đối mặt với <strong data-end="7067" data-start="7054">thử thách</strong>. Một <strong data-end="7087" data-start="7073">môi trường</strong> như vậy giúp mọi người đạt được <strong data-end="7141" data-start="7120">mục tiêu sức khỏe</strong> một cách <strong data-end="7163" data-start="7151">hiệu quả</strong> hơn.)</em></p>

<p data-end="7274" data-start="7174"><strong data-end="7189" data-start="7174">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn tập trung vào vai trò của cộng đồng hỗ trợ, nên tiêu đề này là chuẩn xác.</p>

<hr data-end="7279" data-start="7276">
<h3 data-end="7376" data-start="7281">7. Focusing on sustainable lifestyle changes (<em data-end="7373" data-start="7331">Tập trung vào thay đổi lối sống bền vững</em>)</h3>

<p data-end="7755" data-start="7377">Long-term <strong data-end="7399" data-start="7387">wellness</strong> requires more than just temporary <strong data-end="7443" data-start="7434">diets</strong> or short bursts of <strong data-end="7475" data-start="7463">exercise</strong>. It depends on <strong data-end="7513" data-start="7491">sustainable habits</strong> like better <strong data-end="7535" data-start="7526">sleep</strong>, <strong data-end="7558" data-start="7537">stress management</strong>, and regular <strong data-end="7593" data-start="7572">physical activity</strong>. By setting <strong data-end="7625" data-start="7606">realistic goals</strong> and making gradual <strong data-end="7660" data-start="7645">adjustments</strong>, individuals are more likely to enjoy <strong data-end="7719" data-start="7699">lasting benefits</strong> and a higher <strong data-end="7752" data-start="7733">quality of life</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="8170" data-start="7757"><em data-end="8168" data-start="7757">(<strong data-end="7779" data-start="7759">Sức khỏe lâu dài</strong> đòi hỏi nhiều hơn là chỉ những <strong data-end="7833" data-start="7811">chế độ ăn tạm thời</strong> hoặc các đợt <strong data-end="7860" data-start="7847">tập luyện</strong> ngắn. Nó phụ thuộc vào các <strong data-end="7910" data-start="7888">thói quen bền vững</strong> như <strong data-end="7935" data-start="7915">ngủ nghỉ tốt hơn</strong>, <strong data-end="7959" data-start="7937">quản lý căng thẳng</strong>, và <strong data-end="7999" data-start="7964">hoạt động thể chất thường xuyên</strong>. Bằng cách đặt ra <strong data-end="8038" data-start="8018">mục tiêu thực tế</strong> và thực hiện những <strong data-end="8080" data-start="8058">điều chỉnh dần dần</strong>, mỗi cá nhân sẽ dễ dàng hưởng lợi <strong data-end="8126" data-start="8115">lâu dài</strong> và có <strong data-end="8157" data-start="8133">chất lượng cuộc sống</strong> cao hơn.)</em></p>

<p data-end="8279" data-start="8172"><strong data-end="8187" data-start="8172">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn nói về thói quen bền vững và lợi ích lâu dài, nên tiêu đề này hoàn toàn phù hợp.</p>

<p data-end="1844" data-start="795"><strong>DIGITAL INNOVATION</strong></p>

<ol data-end="8537" data-start="792">
	<li data-end="1844" data-start="792">

	In the digital era, technology has revolutionized the concept of leisure, transforming how individuals relax, interact, and consume entertainment. From on-demand streaming platforms to immersive virtual reality gaming, technology enables highly personalized experiences that cater to diverse preferences. However, this shift also blurs the boundary between work and recreation, as mobile devices and online platforms constantly compete for users’ attention. Redefining leisure in the digital age means balancing technological convenience with the need for offline well-being, ensuring that innovation enhances life quality rather than creating constant digital dependency.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="2955" data-start="1846">
	<p data-end="2955" data-start="1849"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0fe3ce275cb22638b457d][answer][1]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility">Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility</option><option value="Building inclusive and respectful online communities">Building inclusive and respectful online communities</option><option value="Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps">Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps</option><option value="Ongoing concerns about data privacy">Ongoing concerns about data privacy</option><option value="Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs">Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs</option><option value="Promoting essential digital literacy">Promoting essential digital literacy</option><option value="Redefining leisure in the digital era">Redefining leisure in the digital era</option><option value="The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment">The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps ]</label><br data-end="2224" data-start="2221">
	Mobile applications have become powerful enablers of global connectivity, reshaping how people communicate, collaborate, and build relationships. From instant messaging and video conferencing to AI-driven social platforms, apps foster real-time interaction across geographic and cultural boundaries. Beyond personal connections, app ecosystems support professional networking, telemedicine, e-learning, and cross-border commerce. However, this growing reliance also raises challenges, including digital fatigue and increased competition for users’ attention. To maximize their benefits, app developers must focus on designing solutions that prioritize accessibility, inclusivity, and seamless integration into users’ daily lives.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="4087" data-start="2957">
	<p data-end="4087" data-start="2960"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0fe3ce275cb22638b457d][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility">Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility</option><option value="Building inclusive and respectful online communities">Building inclusive and respectful online communities</option><option value="Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps">Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps</option><option value="Ongoing concerns about data privacy">Ongoing concerns about data privacy</option><option value="Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs">Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs</option><option value="Promoting essential digital literacy">Promoting essential digital literacy</option><option value="Redefining leisure in the digital era">Redefining leisure in the digital era</option><option value="The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment">The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Promoting essential digital literacy ]</label><br data-end="3335" data-start="3332">

	<p data-end="5222" data-start="4092"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0fe3ce275cb22638b457d][answer][3]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility">Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility</option><option value="Building inclusive and respectful online communities">Building inclusive and respectful online communities</option><option value="Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps">Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps</option><option value="Ongoing concerns about data privacy">Ongoing concerns about data privacy</option><option value="Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs">Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs</option><option value="Promoting essential digital literacy">Promoting essential digital literacy</option><option value="Redefining leisure in the digital era">Redefining leisure in the digital era</option><option value="The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment">The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment ]</label><br data-end="4467" data-start="4464">
	While technology has enriched entertainment choices, excessive reliance on screen-based activities poses significant health and social challenges. Prolonged exposure to smartphones, video games, and streaming platforms can lead to eye strain, poor sleep quality, reduced physical activity, and shortened attention spans. Socially, individuals risk experiencing isolation when online entertainment replaces meaningful offline connections. Addressing this issue requires a balanced approach: promoting digital well-being, encouraging outdoor recreation, and fostering mindful consumption habits. As technology continues to evolve, society must redefine healthy entertainment practices that maximize benefits without compromising physical or mental health.</p>

	<li data-end="6317" data-start="5224">
	<p data-end="6317" data-start="5227"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68c0fe3ce275cb22638b457d][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility">Balancing innovation with ethical responsibility</option><option value="Building inclusive and respectful online communities">Building inclusive and respectful online communities</option><option value="Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps">Enhancing connectivity with mobile apps</option><option value="Ongoing concerns about data privacy">Ongoing concerns about data privacy</option><option value="Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs">Prioritizing user-friendly and human-centered designs</option><option value="Promoting essential digital literacy">Promoting essential digital literacy</option><option value="Redefining leisure in the digital era">Redefining leisure in the digital era</option><option value="The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment">The risks of excessive screen-based entertainment</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Ongoing concerns about data privacy ]</label><br data-end="5602" data-start="5599">
