<article data-scroll-anchor="false" data-testid="conversation-turn-140" data-turn="assistant" data-turn-id="request-68bd6061-7f98-8320-85c1-68027602356e-1" dir="auto" tabindex="-1">
<h2 data-end="396" data-start="355">The Arrival of the Four-Day Workweek</h2>

<p data-end="440" data-start="397"><em data-end="438" data-start="397">(Sự xuất hiện của tuần làm việc 4 ngày)</em></p>

<hr data-end="445" data-start="442">
<h3 data-end="485" data-start="447">1. A way of life now out of date</h3>

<p data-end="520" data-start="486"><em data-end="518" data-start="486">(Một lối sống nay đã lỗi thời)</em></p>

<p data-end="830" data-start="522">The five-day workweek was first introduced by Henry Ford over a century ago. While it was a revolutionary idea at the time, technology has changed dramatically in the 21st century. Many now believe that this <strong data-end="767" data-start="730">traditional model may be outdated</strong> and it’s time to rethink how we organize our work schedules.</p>

<p data-end="1151" data-start="832"><em data-end="1149" data-start="832">Tuần làm việc 5 ngày được Henry Ford giới thiệu hơn một thế kỷ trước. Dù đó là một ý tưởng mang tính cách mạng vào thời điểm ấy, công nghệ đã thay đổi đáng kể trong thế kỷ 21. Giờ đây, nhiều người tin rằng <strong data-end="1086" data-start="1039">mô hình truyền thống này có thể đã lỗi thời</strong> và đã đến lúc cần suy nghĩ lại về cách tổ chức lịch làm việc.</em></p>

<p data-end="1303" data-start="1153">👉 <strong data-end="1171" data-start="1156">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề phù hợp vì đoạn này nhấn mạnh rằng tuần làm việc 5 ngày – vốn từng là chuẩn mực – nay đã <strong data-end="1281" data-start="1269">lỗi thời</strong> trong bối cảnh mới.</p>

<hr data-end="1308" data-start="1305">
<h3 data-end="1341" data-start="1310">2. Benefits for employees</h3>

<p data-end="1369" data-start="1342"><em data-end="1367" data-start="1342">(Lợi ích cho nhân viên)</em></p>

<p data-end="1645" data-start="1371">An <strong data-end="1391" data-start="1374">extra day off</strong> gives employees more time to spend with their loved ones. It can also <strong data-end="1490" data-start="1462">reduce gender inequality</strong> since women often take on the main role of caring for children. With fewer workdays, they would have more opportunities to balance work and family life.</p>

<p data-end="1937" data-start="1647"><em data-end="1935" data-start="1647">Một <strong data-end="1670" data-start="1652">ngày nghỉ thêm</strong> giúp nhân viên có nhiều thời gian hơn cho những người thân yêu. Nó cũng có thể <strong data-end="1777" data-start="1750">giảm bất bình đẳng giới</strong> vì phụ nữ thường đảm nhận vai trò chính trong việc chăm sóc con cái. Với số ngày làm việc ít hơn, họ sẽ có nhiều cơ hội cân bằng giữa công việc và gia đình.</em></p>

<p data-end="2067" data-start="1939">👉 <strong data-end="1957" data-start="1942">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề phù hợp vì đoạn này liệt kê trực tiếp các <strong data-end="2019" data-start="2008">lợi ích</strong> mà nhân viên nhận được khi có thêm ngày nghỉ.</p>

<h3 data-end="117" data-start="76">3. Undesired financial consequences</h3>

<p data-end="157" data-start="118"><em data-end="155" data-start="118">(Hậu quả tài chính không mong muốn)</em></p>

<p data-end="413" data-start="159">Cutting working hours by 20% can <strong data-end="214" data-start="192">lower productivity</strong> and <strong data-end="243" data-start="219">slow business growth</strong>. This affects <strong data-end="277" data-start="258">company profits</strong>. For instance, when Japan reduced weekly hours from 46 to 30 in 1988, <strong data-end="371" data-start="348">revenue fell by 20%</strong>, showing the risks for business owners.</p>

<p data-end="719" data-start="415"><em data-end="717" data-start="415">Cắt giảm 20% số giờ làm việc có thể <strong data-end="474" data-start="452">làm giảm năng suất</strong> và <strong data-end="513" data-start="478">làm chậm tăng trưởng kinh doanh</strong>. Điều này ảnh hưởng đến <strong data-end="563" data-start="538">lợi nhuận của công ty</strong>. Ví dụ, khi Nhật Bản giảm giờ làm việc hằng tuần từ 46 xuống 30 vào năm 1988, <strong data-end="667" data-start="642">doanh thu đã giảm 20%</strong>, cho thấy những rủi ro đối với chủ doanh nghiệp.</em></p>

<p data-end="846" data-start="721">👉 <strong data-end="739" data-start="724">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề phù hợp vì đoạn này tập trung vào những <strong data-end="818" data-start="788">hậu quả tài chính tiêu cực</strong> của tuần làm việc 4 ngày.</p>

<hr data-end="851" data-start="848">
<h3 data-end="897" data-start="853">4. Unforeseen challenges for employees</h3>

<p data-end="948" data-start="898"><em data-end="946" data-start="898">(Những thách thức ngoài dự kiến cho nhân viên)</em></p>

<p data-end="1273" data-start="950">With fewer days to work, employees must <strong data-end="1037" data-start="990">complete the same tasks in a shorter period</strong>. Some companies saw <strong data-end="1079" data-start="1058">productivity rise</strong> during the first six months, but this was only due to the novelty of the change. Over time, <strong data-end="1194" data-start="1172">stress and burnout</strong> can increase, and companies may even <strong data-end="1251" data-start="1232">lay off workers</strong> who cannot keep up.</p>

<p data-end="1645" data-start="1275"><em data-end="1643" data-start="1275">Khi có ít ngày làm việc hơn, nhân viên phải <strong data-end="1389" data-start="1320">hoàn thành cùng một khối lượng công việc trong thời gian ngắn hơn</strong>. Một số công ty đã chứng kiến <strong data-end="1438" data-start="1420">năng suất tăng</strong> trong sáu tháng đầu tiên, nhưng điều này chỉ là do sự mới mẻ của thay đổi. Về lâu dài, <strong data-end="1552" data-start="1526">căng thẳng và kiệt sức</strong> có thể gia tăng, và công ty thậm chí có thể <strong data-end="1618" data-start="1597">sa thải nhân viên</strong> không theo kịp tiến độ.</em></p>

<p data-end="1789" data-start="1647">👉 <strong data-end="1665" data-start="1650">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề đúng vì đoạn này nhấn mạnh đến <strong data-end="1749" data-start="1705">các thách thức bất ngờ đối với nhân viên</strong> khi phải làm việc với áp lực cao hơn.</p>

<hr data-end="1794" data-start="1791">
<h3 data-end="1836" data-start="1796">5. Difficult to give up bad habits</h3>

<p data-end="1865" data-start="1837"><em data-end="1863" data-start="1837">(Khó từ bỏ thói quen cũ)</em></p>

<p data-end="2174" data-start="1867">Workers are used to a five-day schedule, so having an <strong data-end="1965" data-start="1921">extra day off may feel strange and empty</strong> at first. A study on the “Level of Happiness” found that <strong data-end="2057" data-start="2023">happiness levels remain steady</strong>, meaning that more free time won’t necessarily make them happier. Some may even <strong data-end="2171" data-start="2138">feel bored with nothing to do</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="2549" data-start="2176"><em data-end="2547" data-start="2176">Người lao động đã quen với lịch làm việc 5 ngày, vì vậy việc có <strong data-end="2305" data-start="2241">một ngày nghỉ thêm có thể khiến họ thấy lạ lẫm và trống trải</strong> lúc đầu. Một nghiên cứu về “Mức độ hạnh phúc” cho thấy rằng <strong data-end="2401" data-start="2366">mức độ hạnh phúc vẫn giữ nguyên</strong>, nghĩa là có thêm thời gian rảnh cũng không chắc giúp họ hạnh phúc hơn. Thậm chí, một số người còn <strong data-end="2545" data-start="2501">cảm thấy buồn chán vì không có gì để làm</strong>.</em></p>

<p data-end="2713" data-start="2551">👉 <strong data-end="2569" data-start="2554">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề phù hợp vì đoạn này nói đến việc <strong data-end="2637" data-start="2611">khó từ bỏ thói quen cũ</strong> của tuần làm việc 5 ngày, và thời gian rảnh chưa chắc mang lại hạnh phúc.</p>

<hr data-end="2718" data-start="2715">
<h3 data-end="2759" data-start="2720">6. An unfair plan for some people</h3>

<p data-end="2804" data-start="2760"><em data-end="2802" data-start="2760">(Một kế hoạch bất công cho một số người)</em></p>

<p data-end="3112" data-start="2806">Certain jobs, such as <strong data-end="2840" data-start="2828">teaching</strong>, cannot be reduced since <strong data-end="2920" data-start="2866">students still need the same amount of instruction</strong>. <strong data-end="2958" data-start="2922">Firefighters and police officers</strong> must also continue to work full schedules, as <strong data-end="3053" data-start="3005">emergencies and crime levels do not decrease</strong>. This creates an <strong data-end="3091" data-start="3071">unfair situation</strong> for those workers.</p>

<p data-end="3437" data-start="3114"><em data-end="3435" data-start="3114">Một số công việc, chẳng hạn như <strong data-end="3160" data-start="3147">giảng dạy</strong>, không thể giảm được vì <strong data-end="3228" data-start="3185">học sinh vẫn cần cùng một lượng giờ học</strong>. <strong data-end="3258" data-start="3230">Lính cứu hỏa và cảnh sát</strong> cũng phải tiếp tục làm việc đủ lịch trình, bởi <strong data-end="3359" data-start="3306">các tình huống khẩn cấp và tội phạm không hề giảm</strong>. Điều này tạo nên một <strong data-end="3405" data-start="3382">tình huống bất công</strong> cho những người lao động đó.</em></p>

<p data-end="3573" data-start="3439">👉 <strong data-end="3457" data-start="3442">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề chính xác vì đoạn này mô tả sự <strong data-end="3509" data-start="3497">bất công</strong> khi một số ngành nghề không thể áp dụng tuần làm việc 4 ngày.</p>

<hr data-end="3578" data-start="3575">
<h3 data-end="3628" data-start="3580">7. Alternative solutions worth considering</h3>

<p data-end="3674" data-start="3629"><em data-end="3672" data-start="3629">(Các giải pháp thay thế đáng để cân nhắc)</em></p>

<p data-end="3932" data-start="3676">Instead of moving to a four-day workweek, companies could consider <strong data-end="3760" data-start="3743">other options</strong>. These include <strong data-end="3807" data-start="3776">adding more vacation breaks</strong> or increasing <strong data-end="3841" data-start="3822">“holiday banks”</strong>, which allow employees to take paid leave when needed while keeping a flexible workweek.</p>

<p data-end="4194" data-start="3934"><em data-end="4192" data-start="3934">Thay vì chuyển sang tuần làm việc 4 ngày, các công ty có thể cân nhắc <strong data-end="4026" data-start="4005">các lựa chọn khác</strong>. Chúng bao gồm <strong data-end="4067" data-start="4042">tăng thêm các kỳ nghỉ</strong> hoặc mở rộng <strong data-end="4106" data-start="4081">“ngân hàng ngày nghỉ”</strong>, cho phép nhân viên nghỉ có lương khi cần nhưng vẫn duy trì tuần làm việc linh hoạt.</em></p>

<p data-end="4340" data-start="4196">👉 <strong data-end="4214" data-start="4199">Giải thích:</strong> Tiêu đề phù hợp vì đoạn này giới thiệu <strong data-end="4280" data-start="4254">các giải pháp thay thế</strong> ngoài tuần làm việc 4 ngày để vừa linh hoạt vừa hiệu quả.</p>

<p data-end="307" data-start="281"><strong>Mountains and human connections</strong></p>

<p data-end="746" data-start="119"><strong data-end="359" data-start="119">1. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][0]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Our changing perceptions toward mountains ]</label></strong><br data-end="362" data-start="359">
In the early 1800s, people were believed not to enjoy climbing mountains. Later, as mountain climbing became a popular trend, interest grew rapidly. However, there is evidence that humans have always been fascinated by mountains. The difference now is that people focus mainly on <strong data-end="665" data-start="642">reaching the summit</strong> to admire the majestic views rather than simply exploring the mountain itself.</p>

<p data-end="1388" data-start="753"><strong data-end="993" data-start="753">2. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][1]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ A unique sense of achievement ]</label></strong><br data-end="996" data-start="993">
Climbing to the top of a mountain creates the same <strong data-end="1066" data-start="1047">adrenaline rush</strong> as other extreme sports. But it goes far beyond that. Because of the sheer size and grandeur of mountains, the experience becomes a <strong data-end="1220" data-start="1199">powerful metaphor</strong>, making climbers feel deeply inspired. This intense feeling can even become <strong data-end="1310" data-start="1297">addictive</strong>, as people unconsciously develop a strong desire to keep reaching the peak.</p>

<p data-end="2041" data-start="1395"><strong data-end="1635" data-start="1395">3. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Publicising one's achievements ]</label></strong><br data-end="1638" data-start="1635">
People have always enjoyed capturing and sharing the moment of standing on a mountaintop. This practice existed even <strong data-end="1778" data-start="1755">before social media</strong>, as climbers admired the view or described their experiences to others. With the rise of social media, this trend has become even more common. Now, almost everyone <strong data-end="1982" data-start="1943">takes selfies and posts them online</strong> for friends and family to see after reaching the summit.</p>

<p data-end="2655" data-start="2048"><strong data-end="2288" data-start="2048">4. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][3]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ A wrong priority ]</label></strong><br data-end="2291" data-start="2288">
Recently, some climbers have begun questioning whether this focus on the summit is truly meaningful. The <strong data-end="2420" data-start="2396">most beautiful views</strong> might not be from the peak itself, and the path to the summit is often exhausting, requiring great physical strength. This approach excludes many people and overlooks the beauty found <strong data-end="2631" data-start="2605">all along the mountain</strong>, not just at the top.</p>

<p data-end="3308" data-start="2662"><strong data-end="2902" data-start="2662">5. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ A disturbing revelation ]</label></strong><br data-end="2905" data-start="2902">
A photo taken on <strong data-end="2947" data-start="2922">Mount Everest in 2020</strong>, showing a “<strong data-end="2975" data-start="2960">traffic jam</strong>” of climbers, shocked the world. It revealed how many climbers were rushing to reach the summit during the short window of good weather. This image raised concerns about <strong data-end="3162" data-start="3146">overcrowding</strong> and highlighted how Everest, once seen as a remote and unreachable peak, has now become a site of intense competition and environmental strain.</p>

<p data-end="3920" data-start="3315"><strong data-end="3555" data-start="3315">6. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][5]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ A new focus on sustainability ]</label></strong><br data-end="3558" data-start="3555">
The viral photo made some people feel that climbing Everest had lost its charm. However, mountain climbing itself is not the problem. Instead, climbers must carefully <strong data-end="3762" data-start="3725">reflect on their goals and habits</strong>, ensuring that future <strong data-end="3803" data-start="3785">global tourism</strong> does not negatively impact the environment. A more mindful approach can protect mountains for generations to come.</p>

<p data-end="4556" data-start="3927"><strong data-end="4167" data-start="3927">7. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68bc9686e275cb6b958b456b][answer][6]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A disturbing revelation">A disturbing revelation</option><option value="A new focus on sustainability">A new focus on sustainability</option><option value="A unique sense of achievement">A unique sense of achievement</option><option value="A wrong priority">A wrong priority</option><option value="An intimate relationship">An intimate relationship</option><option value="Our changing perceptions toward mountains">Our changing perceptions toward mountains</option><option value="Publicising one" s="" achievements'="">Publicising one's achievements</option><option value="The history of mountain climbing">The history of mountain climbing</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ An intimate relationship ]</label></strong><br data-end="4170" data-start="4167">
Perhaps we should approach mountains with a <strong data-end="4232" data-start="4214">gentle mindset</strong>, seeing them as companions rather than challenges to conquer. In the 1940 book <em data-end="4333" data-start="4312">The Living Mountain</em> by Shepherd, the author describes climbing near her family farm. She wandered the mountains <strong data-end="4452" data-start="4426">without specific goals</strong>, treating each climb as a <strong data-end="4503" data-start="4479">visit to old friends</strong> instead of a mission to claim victory over nature.</p></div>

	</li>
	<li data-end="458" data-start="382">
	<p data-end="458" data-start="385"><strong data-end="412" data-start="385">A disturbing revelation</strong> → <b>Revelation</b>&nbsp;→ <b>R</b></p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="526" data-start="459">
	<p data-end="526" data-start="462"><strong data-end="495" data-start="462">A new focus on sustainability</strong> → <strong data-end="516" data-start="498">Sustainability</strong> → <strong data-end="524" data-start="519">S</strong></p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="585" data-start="527">
	<p data-end="585" data-start="530"><strong data-end="558" data-start="530">An intimate relationship</strong> → <strong data-end="577" data-start="561">Relationship</strong> → <strong data-end="585" data-start="580">R</strong></p>
	</li>
</ol>

<p data-end="706" data-start="671"><strong data-end="706" data-start="671">"Phương&nbsp;Anh&nbsp;Phung&nbsp;Phí Rổ&nbsp;Sức Rồi."</strong></p>

<ul data-end="1178" data-start="708">
	<li data-end="768" data-start="708">
	<p data-end="768" data-start="710"><strong data-end="722" data-start="710">Phương&nbsp;(P)</strong> → <em data-end="737" data-start="725">Perception</em> – Thay đổi nhận thức về núi.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="829" data-start="769">
	<p data-end="829" data-start="771"><strong data-end="781" data-start="771">Anh&nbsp;(A)</strong> → <em data-end="797" data-start="784">Achievement</em> – Cảm giác thành tựu độc đáo.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="895" data-start="830">
	<p data-end="895" data-start="832"><strong data-end="843" data-start="832">Phung&nbsp;(P)</strong> → <em data-end="857" data-start="846">Publicity</em> – Việc quảng bá thành tích leo núi.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="970" data-start="896">
	<p data-end="970" data-start="898"><strong data-end="909" data-start="898">Phí (P)</strong> → <em data-end="922" data-start="912">Priority</em> – Ưu tiên sai lầm khi chỉ chú trọng đỉnh núi.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="1036" data-start="971">
	<p data-end="1036" data-start="973"><strong data-end="985" data-start="973">Rổ&nbsp;(R)</strong> → <i>Revelation</i>&nbsp;– Những tiết lộ gây sốc, ví dụ hình ảnh tắc nghẽn trên núi Everest.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="1108" data-start="1037">
	<p data-end="1108" data-start="1039"><strong data-end="1050" data-start="1039">Sức (S)</strong> → <em data-end="1069" data-start="1053">Sustainability</em> – Tập trung vào phát triển bền vững.</p>
	</li>
	<li data-end="1178" data-start="1109">
	<p data-end="1178" data-start="1111"><strong data-end="1122" data-start="1111">Rồi&nbsp;(R)</strong> → <em data-end="1139" data-start="1125">Relationship</em> – Mối quan hệ gắn bó, gần gũi với núi.</p>
	</li>
</ul>

<p data-end="562" data-start="462">Còn ae muốn học kỹ năng làm bài thì như sau:</p>

<h3 data-end="263" data-start="213">1. Our changing perceptions toward mountains&nbsp;(<em data-end="304" data-start="264">Nhận thức thay đổi của chúng ta về núi)</em></h3>

<p data-end="721" data-start="308"><br data-end="329" data-start="326">
In the early 1800s, people were believed not to enjoy climbing mountains. Later, as mountain climbing became a popular trend, interest grew rapidly. However, there is evidence that humans have always been fascinated by mountains. The difference now is that people focus mainly on reaching the <strong data-end="632" data-start="622">summit</strong> to admire the majestic <strong data-end="665" data-start="656">views</strong> rather than simply exploring the <strong data-end="711" data-start="699">mountain</strong> itself.</p>

<p data-end="1139" data-start="723"><em data-end="1137" data-start="723">(Vào đầu những năm 1800, người ta tin rằng con người không thích leo núi. Sau này, khi leo núi trở thành một xu hướng phổ biến, sự quan tâm đã tăng nhanh chóng. Tuy nhiên, có bằng chứng cho thấy con người luôn bị cuốn hút bởi <strong data-end="957" data-start="950">núi</strong>. Sự khác biệt hiện nay là mọi người chủ yếu tập trung vào việc chinh phục <strong data-end="1044" data-start="1032">đỉnh núi</strong> để chiêm ngưỡng <strong data-end="1075" data-start="1061">quang cảnh</strong> hùng vĩ thay vì chỉ đơn giản là khám phá bản thân ngọn núi).</em></p>

<p data-end="1291" data-start="1141"><strong data-end="1156" data-start="1141">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn so sánh nhận thức trước đây và hiện tại của con người về núi, nên tiêu đề về <em data-end="1272" data-start="1243">sự thay đổi trong nhận thức</em> là phù hợp nhất.</p>

<hr data-end="1296" data-start="1293">
<h3 data-end="1336" data-start="1298">2. A unique sense of achievement&nbsp;(<em data-end="1365" data-start="1337">Cảm giác thành tựu độc đáo)</em></h3>

<p data-end="1802" data-start="1369">Nội dung đoạn văn:<br data-end="1390" data-start="1387">
Climbing to the top of a <strong data-end="1427" data-start="1415">mountain</strong> creates the same <strong data-end="1464" data-start="1445">adrenaline rush</strong> as other extreme sports. But it goes far beyond that. Because of the sheer size and <strong data-end="1561" data-start="1549">grandeur</strong> of mountains, the experience becomes a powerful <strong data-end="1622" data-start="1610">metaphor</strong>, making climbers feel deeply <strong data-end="1664" data-start="1652">inspired</strong>. This intense feeling can even become <strong data-end="1716" data-start="1703">addictive</strong>, as people unconsciously develop a strong <strong data-end="1769" data-start="1759">desire</strong> to keep reaching the <strong data-end="1799" data-start="1791">peak</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="2217" data-start="1804"><em data-end="2215" data-start="1804">(Leo lên đỉnh <strong data-end="1826" data-start="1819">núi</strong> mang lại sự <strong data-end="1852" data-start="1839">hưng phấn</strong> giống như các môn thể thao mạo hiểm khác. Nhưng nó còn vượt xa hơn thế. Bởi vì kích thước và <strong data-end="1960" data-start="1946">vẻ hùng vĩ</strong> của núi, trải nghiệm này trở thành một <strong data-end="2009" data-start="2000">ẩn dụ</strong> mạnh mẽ, khiến người leo núi cảm thấy vô cùng <strong data-end="2068" data-start="2056">cảm hứng</strong>. Cảm giác mãnh liệt này thậm chí có thể trở nên <strong data-end="2131" data-start="2117">gây nghiện</strong>, khi con người vô thức nuôi dưỡng <strong data-end="2179" data-start="2166">khát vọng</strong> tiếp tục chinh phục <strong data-end="2212" data-start="2200">đỉnh núi</strong>.)</em></p>

<p data-end="2347" data-start="2219"><strong data-end="2234" data-start="2219">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn nói về cảm xúc mạnh mẽ và đặc biệt khi leo núi, nên phù hợp với tiêu đề <em data-end="2344" data-start="2316">cảm giác thành tựu độc đáo</em>.</p>

<hr data-end="2352" data-start="2349">
<h3 data-end="2393" data-start="2354">3. Publicising one’s achievements&nbsp;(<em data-end="2422" data-start="2394">Quảng bá thành tựu cá nhân)</em></h3>

<p data-end="2882" data-start="2426"><br data-end="2447" data-start="2444">
People have always enjoyed <strong data-end="2487" data-start="2474">capturing</strong> and <strong data-end="2503" data-start="2492">sharing</strong> the moment of standing on a <strong data-end="2547" data-start="2532">mountaintop</strong>. This practice existed even before <strong data-end="2599" data-start="2583">social media</strong>, as climbers admired the <strong data-end="2633" data-start="2625">view</strong> or described their <strong data-end="2668" data-start="2653">experiences</strong> to others. With the rise of <strong data-end="2713" data-start="2697">social media</strong>, this trend has become even more common. Now, almost everyone takes <strong data-end="2793" data-start="2782">selfies</strong> and <strong data-end="2807" data-start="2798">posts</strong> them online for friends and family to see after reaching the <strong data-end="2879" data-start="2869">summit</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="3306" data-start="2884"><em data-end="3304" data-start="2884">(Con người luôn thích <strong data-end="2918" data-start="2907">ghi lại</strong> và <strong data-end="2933" data-start="2922">chia sẻ</strong> khoảnh khắc đứng trên <strong data-end="2968" data-start="2956">đỉnh núi</strong>. Thói quen này đã tồn tại từ trước thời <strong data-end="3024" data-start="3009">mạng xã hội</strong>, khi người leo núi ngắm cảnh hoặc kể lại <strong data-end="3081" data-start="3066">trải nghiệm</strong> của mình. Với sự phát triển của <strong data-end="3129" data-start="3114">mạng xã hội</strong>, xu hướng này càng trở nên phổ biến. Giờ đây, hầu như ai cũng chụp <strong data-end="3213" data-start="3197">ảnh tự sướng</strong> và <strong data-end="3229" data-start="3217">đăng tải</strong> lên mạng để bạn bè và gia đình cùng xem sau khi chinh phục <strong data-end="3301" data-start="3289">đỉnh núi</strong>.)</em></p>

<p data-end="3446" data-start="3308"><strong data-end="3323" data-start="3308">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn tập trung vào việc chia sẻ khoảnh khắc và thành tích leo núi, nên tiêu đề <em data-end="3435" data-start="3407">quảng bá thành tựu cá nhân</em> là đúng.</p>

<hr data-end="3451" data-start="3448">
<h3 data-end="3478" data-start="3453">4. A wrong priority (<em data-end="3500" data-start="3479">Một ưu tiên sai lầm)</em></h3>

<p data-end="3917" data-start="3504"><br data-end="3525" data-start="3522">
Recently, some climbers have begun questioning whether this focus on the <strong data-end="3608" data-start="3598">summit</strong> is truly meaningful. The most beautiful <strong data-end="3658" data-start="3649">views</strong> might not be from the <strong data-end="3689" data-start="3681">peak</strong> itself, and the path to the summit is often <strong data-end="3748" data-start="3734">exhausting</strong>, requiring great physical <strong data-end="3787" data-start="3775">strength</strong>. This approach <strong data-end="3815" data-start="3803">excludes</strong> many people and overlooks the <strong data-end="3856" data-start="3846">beauty</strong> found all along the <strong data-end="3889" data-start="3877">mountain</strong>, not just at the <strong data-end="3914" data-start="3907">top</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="4326" data-start="3919"><em data-end="4324" data-start="3919">(Gần đây, một số người leo núi bắt đầu đặt câu hỏi liệu việc tập trung quá nhiều vào <strong data-end="4017" data-start="4005">đỉnh núi</strong> có thực sự ý nghĩa. Những <strong data-end="4058" data-start="4044">quang cảnh</strong> đẹp nhất có thể không nằm ở chính <strong data-end="4101" data-start="4093">đỉnh</strong> đó, và con đường leo lên thường vô cùng <strong data-end="4153" data-start="4142">mệt mỏi</strong>, đòi hỏi nhiều <strong data-end="4181" data-start="4169">sức mạnh</strong> thể chất. Cách tiếp cận này khiến nhiều người bị <strong data-end="4242" data-start="4231">loại bỏ</strong> và bỏ qua <strong data-end="4263" data-start="4253">vẻ đẹp</strong> trải dài khắp <strong data-end="4290" data-start="4278">ngọn núi</strong>, chứ không chỉ ở <strong data-end="4321" data-start="4308">trên đỉnh</strong>.)</em></p>

<p data-end="4446" data-start="4328"><strong data-end="4343" data-start="4328">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn cho rằng việc quá chú trọng vào đỉnh núi là sai lầm, nên tiêu đề <em data-end="4435" data-start="4418">ưu tiên sai lầm</em> phù hợp.</p>

<hr data-end="4451" data-start="4448">
<h3 data-end="4485" data-start="4453">5. A disturbing revelation&nbsp;(<em data-end="4512" data-start="4486">Một sự thật đáng lo ngại)</em></h3>

<p data-end="4514" data-start="4486"><br data-end="4537" data-start="4534">
A <strong data-end="4548" data-start="4539">photo</strong> taken on <strong data-end="4575" data-start="4558">Mount Everest</strong> in 2020, showing a “traffic jam” of <strong data-end="4624" data-start="4612">climbers</strong>, shocked the <strong data-end="4647" data-start="4638">world</strong>. It revealed how many climbers were <strong data-end="4695" data-start="4684">rushing</strong> to reach the <strong data-end="4719" data-start="4709">summit</strong> during the short window of good <strong data-end="4763" data-start="4752">weather</strong>. This <strong data-end="4779" data-start="4770">image</strong> raised concerns about <strong data-end="4818" data-start="4802">overcrowding</strong> and highlighted how Everest, once seen as a remote and <strong data-end="4894" data-start="4874">unreachable peak</strong>, has now become a site of intense <strong data-end="4944" data-start="4929">competition</strong> and environmental <strong data-end="4973" data-start="4963">strain</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="5462" data-start="4978"><em data-end="5460" data-start="4978">(Một <strong data-end="4995" data-start="4984">bức ảnh</strong> chụp trên <strong data-end="5017" data-start="5006">Everest</strong> năm 2020, cho thấy cảnh “tắc nghẽn” của những <strong data-end="5081" data-start="5064">người leo núi</strong>, đã khiến cả <strong data-end="5107" data-start="5095">thế giới</strong> sửng sốt. Nó phơi bày việc quá nhiều người đang <strong data-end="5165" data-start="5156">đổ xô</strong> lên <strong data-end="5178" data-start="5170">đỉnh</strong> trong khoảng thời gian ngắn có <strong data-end="5223" data-start="5210">thời tiết</strong> thuận lợi. <strong data-end="5247" data-start="5235">Hình ảnh</strong> này dấy lên lo ngại về tình trạng <strong data-end="5293" data-start="5282">quá tải</strong> và cho thấy Everest, vốn từng được coi là một <strong data-end="5378" data-start="5340">đỉnh núi xa xôi không thể chạm tới</strong>, nay đã trở thành nơi của sự <strong data-end="5422" data-start="5408">cạnh tranh</strong> khốc liệt và <strong data-end="5446" data-start="5436">sức ép</strong> môi trường.)</em></p>

<p data-end="5602" data-start="5464"><strong data-end="5479" data-start="5464">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn nhắc đến bức ảnh gây sốc, tiết lộ thực trạng đáng lo ngại, nên tiêu đề <em data-end="5586" data-start="5560">một sự thật đáng lo ngại</em> là chính xác.</p>

<hr data-end="5607" data-start="5604">
<h3 data-end="5647" data-start="5609">6. A new focus on sustainability (<em data-end="5688" data-start="5648">Một sự tập trung mới vào tính bền vững)</em></h3>

<p data-end="5690" data-start="5648"><br data-end="5713" data-start="5710">
The viral <strong data-end="5732" data-start="5723">photo</strong> made some people feel that climbing <strong data-end="5780" data-start="5769">Everest</strong> had lost its <strong data-end="5803" data-start="5794">charm</strong>. However, mountain climbing itself is not the <strong data-end="5861" data-start="5850">problem</strong>. Instead, climbers must carefully <strong data-end="5907" data-start="5896">reflect</strong> on their <strong data-end="5926" data-start="5917">goals</strong> and <strong data-end="5941" data-start="5931">habits</strong>, ensuring that future global <strong data-end="5982" data-start="5971">tourism</strong> does not negatively <strong data-end="6013" data-start="6003">impact</strong> the <strong data-end="6033" data-start="6018">environment</strong>. A more <strong data-end="6053" data-start="6042">mindful</strong> approach can <strong data-end="6078" data-start="6067">protect</strong> mountains for generations to come.</p>

<p data-end="6554" data-start="6117"><em data-end="6552" data-start="6117">(Bức <strong data-end="6130" data-start="6123">ảnh</strong> lan truyền khiến một số người cảm thấy việc chinh phục <strong data-end="6197" data-start="6186">Everest</strong> đã mất đi <strong data-end="6223" data-start="6208">sức hấp dẫn</strong>. Tuy nhiên, chính việc leo núi không phải là <strong data-end="6279" data-start="6269">vấn đề</strong>. Thay vào đó, người leo núi cần <strong data-end="6324" data-start="6312">suy ngẫm</strong> cẩn thận về <strong data-end="6349" data-start="6337">mục tiêu</strong> và <strong data-end="6366" data-start="6353">thói quen</strong>, để đảm bảo rằng <strong data-end="6395" data-start="6384">du lịch</strong> toàn cầu trong tương lai không gây <strong data-end="6444" data-start="6431">ảnh hưởng</strong> xấu đến <strong data-end="6467" data-start="6453">môi trường</strong>. Một cách tiếp cận <strong data-end="6500" data-start="6487">có ý thức</strong> hơn có thể <strong data-end="6522" data-start="6512">bảo vệ</strong> núi non cho các thế hệ sau.)</em></p>

<p data-end="6703" data-start="6556"><strong data-end="6571" data-start="6556">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn hướng sự chú ý đến việc bảo vệ môi trường và phát triển bền vững, nên tiêu đề <em data-end="6692" data-start="6659">tập trung mới vào tính bền vững</em> là đúng.</p>

<hr data-end="6708" data-start="6705">
<h3 data-end="6743" data-start="6710">7. An intimate relationship&nbsp;(<em data-end="6769" data-start="6744">Một mối quan hệ gần gũi)</em></h3>

<p data-end="6771" data-start="6744"><br data-end="6794" data-start="6791">
Perhaps we should approach <strong data-end="6834" data-start="6821">mountains</strong> with a gentle <strong data-end="6860" data-start="6849">mindset</strong>, seeing them as <strong data-end="6891" data-start="6877">companions</strong> rather than <strong data-end="6918" data-start="6904">challenges</strong> to <strong data-end="6933" data-start="6922">conquer</strong>. In the 1940 book <em data-end="6973" data-start="6952">The Living Mountain</em> by Shepherd, the <strong data-end="7001" data-start="6991">author</strong> describes climbing near her family <strong data-end="7045" data-start="7037">farm</strong>. She <strong data-end="7063" data-start="7051">wandered</strong> the <strong data-end="7081" data-start="7068">mountains</strong> without specific <strong data-end="7108" data-start="7099">goals</strong>, treating each <strong data-end="7133" data-start="7124">climb</strong> as a <strong data-end="7148" data-start="7139">visit</strong> to old <strong data-end="7167" data-start="7156">friends</strong> instead of a <strong data-end="7192" data-start="7181">mission</strong> to claim <strong data-end="7213" data-start="7202">victory</strong> over <strong data-end="7229" data-start="7219">nature</strong>.</p>

<p data-end="7747" data-start="7234"><em data-end="7745" data-start="7234">(Có lẽ chúng ta nên tiếp cận <strong data-end="7271" data-start="7264">núi</strong> với một <strong data-end="7291" data-start="7280">tâm thế</strong> nhẹ nhàng, coi chúng như những <strong data-end="7346" data-start="7323">người bạn đồng hành</strong> thay vì là <strong data-end="7371" data-start="7358">thử thách</strong> để <strong data-end="7389" data-start="7375">chinh phục</strong>. Trong cuốn sách <em data-end="7428" data-start="7407">The Living Mountain</em> năm 1940 của Shepherd, <strong data-end="7463" data-start="7452">tác giả</strong> mô tả việc leo núi gần <strong data-end="7500" data-start="7487">nông trại</strong> gia đình bà. Bà đã <strong data-end="7534" data-start="7520">lang thang</strong> trên những <strong data-end="7558" data-start="7546">ngọn núi</strong> mà không đặt ra <strong data-end="7587" data-start="7575">mục tiêu</strong> cụ thể, coi mỗi lần <strong data-end="7619" data-start="7608">leo núi</strong> như một <strong data-end="7643" data-start="7628">cuộc gặp gỡ</strong> với những <strong data-end="7670" data-start="7654">người bạn cũ</strong> thay vì một <strong data-end="7695" data-start="7683">nhiệm vụ</strong> để giành <strong data-end="7720" data-start="7705">chiến thắng</strong> trước <strong data-end="7742" data-start="7727">thiên nhiên</strong>.)</em></p>

<p data-end="7876" data-start="7749"><strong data-end="7764" data-start="7749">Giải thích:</strong> Đoạn văn thể hiện mối gắn bó thân tình giữa con người và núi, nên tiêu đề <em data-end="7860" data-start="7839">mối quan hệ gần gũi</em> là chính xác.</p>

            <div class="font-weight-600">[Mai Hien key 6.0] - Reading part 4 - The early Australians</div>
            <div><p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><strong>Read the passage quickly. Choose a heading for each numbered paragraph (1-7) from the drop-down box.</strong></span></p>

<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><strong>The early Australians</strong></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">1. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][0]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resettlement">Natural barrier to resettlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ An alternative history to the settlement ]</label></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">1. The history of early Australians stretches back much further than previously believed, with evidence suggesting human presence on the Australian continent dating back approximately 65,000 years. This timeline challenges traditional views held by historians regarding the first human settlers in Australia. Carbon analysis of archaeological sites has provided different results, leading to alternative hypotheses about the early inhabitants of the land Down Under. The findings shed new light on the ancient origins and rich cultural heritage of the Indigenous people who have inhabited the continent for millennia.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">2.&nbsp;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][1]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resttlement">Natural barrier to resttlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Natural barrier to resttlement ]</label></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">2. Recent discoveries have revealed that the settlement of Australia was not a singular event. In addition to the early settlers, scientists have uncovered traces of two other human groups that migrated to the continent. The presence of multiple groups suggests a complex history of human migration and interaction. However, reaching the isolated continent would have posed significant challenges for ancient humans, as they would have needed to traverse vast stretches of open sea, a feat seemingly impossible with the technology available to them at the time.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">3.&nbsp;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resettlement">Natural barrier to resettlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets ]</label></span></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">3. The aid of advanced equipment and techniques has allowed scientists to identify a series of small islands closely connected, forming a continuous pathway leading to Australia. Remote sensing technology has helped researchers identify and map small islands and potential migration routes. Geographic Information Systems (GIS) have integrated various data sets, to discover about the past migration corridors. This discovery provides insight into the probable routes taken by ancient migrants as they ventured across the vast expanse of the sea, providing a deeper understanding of the complex migration patterns that shaped the early history of the continent.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">4.&nbsp;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][3]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resettlement">Natural barrier to resettlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ A journey made in stages ]</label></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">4. The migration patterns of early Australians reveal a gradual journey to the continent. Archaeological evidence points to the likelihood of different tribes arriving in Australia through a series of island-hopping journeys. Each island served as a resting point and a source of food, allowing them to continue their voyage. This gradual movement indicates an adaptive and resourceful approach taken by these ancient tribes, who navigated the challenges of the terrain to ultimately settle in Australia.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">5.&nbsp;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resettlement">Natural barrier to resettlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ A new evidence that leads to speculation ]</label></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">5. Scientists can only speculate about the exact number of individuals required to undertake such a migration, which could have ranged from a small group to several thousand people. The uncertainty stems from various factors, including the limitations of available archaeological evidence and the complexities of ancient human migration. The lack of exact statistics makes it challenging to determine the scale and composition of these early human journeys accurately. However, ongoing research and technological advancements may offer more insights in the future.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">6.&nbsp;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][5]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resettlement">Natural barrier to resettlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Lacking both knowledge and skills ]</label></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">6. Some skeptics argue that ancient humans didn’t have enough the intellectual capacity, knowledge, and skills needed to undertake such journeys. They question whether early humans possessed the navigational and maritime expertise to traverse vast stretches of ocean. Critics contend that without advanced tools or navigational aids, navigating through open seas would have been beyond the capabilities of ancient civilizations. However, it is crucial to acknowledge that human ingenuity and adaptability have proven remarkable throughout history, enabling our ancestors to overcome various challenges and achieve extraordinary feats.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">7.&nbsp;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;"><select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6792e60be275cbe5a78e2e66][answer][6]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A journey made in stages">A journey made in stages</option><option value="A new evidence that leads to speculation">A new evidence that leads to speculation</option><option value="An alternative history to the settlement">An alternative history to the settlement</option><option value="Lacking both knowledge and skills">Lacking both knowledge and skills</option><option value="Natural barrier to resettlement">Natural barrier to resettlement</option><option value="Technology helps uncover the ocean" s="" secrets'="">Technology helps uncover the ocean's secrets</option><option value="The determination of the explorer in ages">The determination of the explorer in ages</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ The determination of the explorer in ages ]</label></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;">7. History has demonstrated the unwavering determination and resilience of human explorers in the past. From deep-sea expeditions in ancient times to modern space travel, humans have showcased their resolve to explore and conquer the unknown. The same determination might have driven the early Australians to embark on perilous journeys across treacherous waters. While the challenges they faced were undoubtedly immense, the spirit of human curiosity and the desire to discover new lands and opportunities likely motivated these ancient explorers, leaving a remarkable legacy in the annals of history.</span></p></div>

		(Họ đặt câu hỏi liệu con người thời đó có sở hữu đủ chuyên môn về hàng hải và định hướng để vượt qua những vùng biển rộng lớn hay không.)</em></li>
	</ul>
	</li>

		<li><em><strong>Trích dẫn</strong>: "From deep-sea expeditions in ancient times to modern space travel, humans have showcased their resolve to explore and conquer the unknown."<br>
		(Từ các cuộc thám hiểm biển sâu thời cổ đại đến du hành không gian hiện đại, con người đã thể hiện quyết tâm khám phá và chinh phục những điều chưa biết.)</em></li>
	</ul>

    <div class="w3-padding w3-light-grey ">

        <div class="title-quiz-choice my-3">
            <div class="font-weight-600">[Mai Hien key 6.0] - Reading part 4 - Frozen Antarctica</div>
            <div><p><b>Read the text. Match the headings to the paragraphs. There is one heading that you will not use.</b></p>

<p><b>Frozen Antarctica</b></p>

<p>1. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][0]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Who is in charge ]</label></p>

<p>1. This continent is governed by an international agreement known as the Antarctic Treaty System, established in 1961. This treaty ensures that the region is utilized for peaceful purposes and encourages global scientific collaboration. While no nation officially owns this land, several countries-Argentina, Australia, Chile, France, New Zealand, Norway, and the United Kingdom-assert territorial claims. The treaty forbids military activity, resource extraction, and nuclear tests, designating the area for research and conservation efforts. As a result, scientists from various countries gather to study this unique environment, sharing their discoveries for the benefit of humanity.</p>

<p>2.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][1]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ First step on the ice ]</label></p>

<p>2. Setting foot on Antarctica is a significant event for any explorer or scientist. The journey typically begins in South America, where travelers board a ship or a plane to cross the Drake Passage. Once they arrive, the first step on the ice is both exhilarating and daunting. Visitors are immediately struck by the vast expanse of white, the crisp, cold air, and the breathtaking scenery. The sound of crunching ice underfoot serves as a reminder of the remote and untouched nature of this continent, a place where human footprints are few and far between.</p>

<p>3.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Where is the end of the earth ]</label></p>

<p>3. Positioned around the South Pole, Antarctica represents the southernmost point on the planet. The continent's remoteness contributes to its mystique, drawing adventurers and researchers alike. The harsh conditions, including bitter cold and relentless winds, create a sense of otherworldliness. In many ways, it feels like the last frontier on Earth, where the landscape remains largely unspoiled and the natural world thrives in its purest form</p>

<p>4.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][3]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Hidden geography ]</label></p>

<p>4. Beneath the massive ice sheets lies a concealed landscape that reveals much about the planet's geological history. This region hosts the largest ice mass globally, covering approximately 98 percent of its area. The ice conceals a variety of geological features, including mountains and valleys. Researchers analyze ice cores extracted from deep within the layers to uncover details about past climates and atmospheric conditions. These investigations provide vital information for understanding global climate change and its potential implications for our world.</p>

<p>5.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Race to the pole ]</label></p>

<p>5. The pursuit of the southernmost point in the early 20th century captivated many. Adventurers such as Robert Falcon Scott and Roald Amundsen undertook perilous journeys to achieve this milestone. Amundsen's successful expedition in 1911 marked a significant achievement in exploration, while Scott's tragic story underscored the risks associated with such endeavors. These tales of courage and ambition continue to inspire modern explorers, highlighting the fascination that this harsh terrain holds.</p>

<p>6.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][5]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Less effort needed ]</label></p>

<p>6. Recent advancements in technology have made reaching this icy expanse easier than in the past. Modern icebreakers and advanced aircraft enable safer and more efficient travel. This accessibility has led to a rise in interest for tourism, allowing more people to experience the breathtaking beauty of the landscape. However, the increase in visitors raises concerns about the potential environmental impact, emphasizing the necessity for sustainable practices to safeguard this delicate ecosystem.</p>

<p>7.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[6790c020e275cb8d6c8e2dd2][answer][6]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="First step on the ice">First step on the ice</option><option value="Hidden geography">Hidden geography</option><option value="Less effort needed">Less effort needed</option><option value="Race to the pole">Race to the pole</option><option value="Where is the end of the earth">Where is the end of the earth</option><option value="Who is in charge">Who is in charge</option><option value="Why is it so cold">Why is it so cold</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Why is it so cold ]</label></p>

<p>7. The extreme low temperatures in this region result mainly from its high elevation and geographic positioning. Being located over the South Pole means it receives minimal direct sunlight, especially during the prolonged winter months of darkness. Average temperatures can plummet below -60°C (-76°F), with summer still remaining quite frigid. The reflective nature of ice further contributes to the chilling climate. Understanding these climatic influences is crucial for scientists studying global weather systems and shifts in climate patterns.</p></div>
        </div>
    </div>

2. First step on the ice<br>
3. Where is the end of the earth<br>
4. Hidden geography<br>
5. Race to the pole<br>
6.. Less effort needed<br>
7. Why is it so cold</em></p>

<p><em><strong>Giải thích:</strong></em></p>

<ol>
	<li><em><b><span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">Who </span>is in charge (Ai chịu trách nhiệm)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này nói về hệ thống Hiệp ước Nam Cực và các quốc gia tuyên bố chủ quyền lãnh thổ, nhưng không có quốc gia nào sở hữu chính thức lục địa này.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "This continent is governed by an international agreement known as the Antarctic Treaty System." (Lục địa này được quản lý bởi một thỏa thuận quốc tế gọi là Hệ thống Hiệp ước Nam Cực.)</em></li>
	<li><em><b><span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">First step</span> on the ice (Bước chân đầu tiên lên băng)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này mô tả cảm giác của các nhà thám hiểm và nhà khoa học khi lần đầu tiên đặt chân lên Nam Cực.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "The first step on the ice is both exhilarating and daunting." (Bước chân đầu tiên lên băng vừa thú vị vừa đầy thử thách.)</em></li>
	<li><em><b>Where is the end of the <span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">earth</span> (Nơi tận cùng của trái đất)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này nói về vị trí của Nam Cực, là điểm cực nam của hành tinh và sự bí ẩn của lục địa này.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "Positioned around the South Pole, Antarctica represents the southernmost point on the planet." (Nằm xung quanh Cực Nam, Nam Cực đại diện cho điểm cực nam của hành tinh.)</em></li>
	<li><em><b>Hidden <span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">geography </span>(Địa lý ẩn giấu)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này nói về cảnh quan dưới lớp băng của Nam Cực, bao gồm những dãy núi và thung lũng, cùng với nghiên cứu về khí hậu trong quá khứ.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "Beneath the massive ice sheets lies a concealed landscape that reveals much about the planet's geological history." (Beneath the massive ice sheets lies a concealed landscape that reveals much about the planet's geological history.)</em></li>
	<li><em><b><span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">Race </span>to the pole (Cuộc đua đến cực)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này kể về cuộc đua của các nhà thám hiểm trong thế kỷ 20 để đến được điểm cực nam của hành tinh, đặc biệt là các cuộc thám hiểm của Robert Falcon Scott và Roald Amundsen.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "Adventurers such as Robert Falcon Scott and Roald Amundsen undertook perilous journeys to achieve this milestone." (Những nhà thám hiểm như Robert Falcon Scott và Roald Amundsen đã thực hiện những cuộc hành trình nguy hiểm để đạt được cột mốc này.)</em></li>
	<li><em><b><span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">Less </span>effort needed (Ít nỗ lực hơn cần thiết)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này nói về sự tiến bộ trong công nghệ giúp việc di chuyển đến Nam Cực trở nên dễ dàng hơn, cũng như sự gia tăng du lịch và những tác động môi trường.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "Recent advancements in technology have made reaching this icy expanse easier than in the past." (Những tiến bộ gần đây trong công nghệ đã làm cho việc tiếp cận vùng băng này trở nên dễ dàng hơn so với trước.)</em></li>
	<li><em><b>Why is it so <span style="background-color:#e74c3c;">cold </span>(Tại sao lại lạnh như vậy)</b><br>
	Giải thích: Đoạn này giải thích nguyên nhân của cái lạnh cực độ ở Nam Cực, bao gồm độ cao, vị trí địa lý và băng tuyết.<br>
	Trích dẫn: "The extreme low temperatures in this region result mainly from its high elevation and geographic positioning." (Nhiệt độ thấp cực độ ở khu vực này chủ yếu là do độ cao và vị trí địa lý của nó.)</em></li>
</ol>

<p>1. <select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68cb875ee275cbca628b457e][answer][0]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A long career showing exceptional ability">A long career showing exceptional ability</option><option value="Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer">Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer</option><option value="Attempting to create a gender balance">Attempting to create a gender balance</option><option value="Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics">Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics</option><option value="Gender obscures achievements">Gender obscures achievements</option><option value="Labels can change perspective on people">Labels can change perspective on people</option><option value="Men unfairly credited">Men unfairly credited</option><option value="Uniformity as a Disadvantage">Uniformity as a Disadvantage</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Gender obscures achievements ]</label><br data-end="896" data-start="893">

<p>3.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68cb875ee275cbca628b457e][answer][2]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A long career showing exceptional ability">A long career showing exceptional ability</option><option value="Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer">Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer</option><option value="Attempting to create a gender balance">Attempting to create a gender balance</option><option value="Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics">Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics</option><option value="Gender obscures achievements">Gender obscures achievements</option><option value="Labels can change perspective on people">Labels can change perspective on people</option><option value="Men unfairly credited">Men unfairly credited</option><option value="Uniformity as a Disadvantage">Uniformity as a Disadvantage</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Men unfairly credited ]</label><br data-end="1952" data-start="1949">

<p>5.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68cb875ee275cbca628b457e][answer][4]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A long career showing exceptional ability">A long career showing exceptional ability</option><option value="Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer">Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer</option><option value="Attempting to create a gender balance">Attempting to create a gender balance</option><option value="Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics">Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics</option><option value="Gender obscures achievements">Gender obscures achievements</option><option value="Labels can change perspective on people">Labels can change perspective on people</option><option value="Men unfairly credited">Men unfairly credited</option><option value="Uniformity as a Disadvantage">Uniformity as a Disadvantage</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Labels can change perspective on people ]</label><br data-end="2946" data-start="2943">

<p>6.&nbsp;<select class="select_word" name="Quiz[68cb875ee275cbca628b457e][answer][5]" disabled=""><option value="">----</option><option value="A long career showing exceptional ability">A long career showing exceptional ability</option><option value="Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer">Acknowledging achievement of a pioneer</option><option value="Attempting to create a gender balance">Attempting to create a gender balance</option><option value="Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics">Extra heading: Public interest in mathematics</option><option value="Gender obscures achievements">Gender obscures achievements</option><option value="Labels can change perspective on people">Labels can change perspective on people</option><option value="Men unfairly credited">Men unfairly credited</option><option value="Uniformity as a Disadvantage">Uniformity as a Disadvantage</option></select><label class="text-error" style="width: 20px; line-height: 4px"></label><label class="text-success word_success" style="display: inline; margin: 0 8px;">[ Attempting to create a gender balance ]</label><br data-end="3450" data-start="3447">
